PHYOGS DRAG PO'I DPUNG SBYOR MI BZAD PA'I DBANG GIS GANGS LJONGS
GDAN SA GSUM

GYI CHOS BYED SLOB GNYER BA MANG PO RGYA GAR SA THOG TU PHEBS
'BYOR RNAMS ^ GONG SA ^ SKYABS MGON CHEN PO'I THUGS BSKYED MDZAD
BZANG RMAD BYUNG DANG, RGYA GAR GZHUNG SOGS KYI 'TSO SKYOB ROGS
MGON BLA MED KYI BKRIN

LAS BHAG SAR PHYOGS BSDUS SLOB GNYER MDZAD MUS KYANG, GZIGS DPE
RIGS HA CANG DKON GSHIS SHAR CHEN NGAG DBANG TSUL KHRIMS KYIS
MDZAD PA'I 'DUL SDOM 'DI NYID SER SMAD GRA TSANG KHONGS PHAG RI
KHAM BU

DON LDAN KHANG GSAR BA'I MI NGO BLO BZANG DON LDAN NAS LHAG BSAM
DAG PAS YON SBYAR TE KA SBUG MA nI PI RIN tING WARKAS DPAR KHANG
DU DPAR BSKRUN BGYIS PA'I DGE BSNGO'I SMON TSIG TU YONGS 'DZIN
KHRI BYANG SKYE MING PAS
